## Method

```
Pages: curl -s -o /dev/null -L -m 15 -w "%{http_code}\n" <url>   (xargs -P 24)
Imgs:  curl -s -o /dev/null    -m 15 -w "%{http_code}|%{size_download}\n" <url>   (xargs -P 32)
```
